# Opportunity in nonProfitForSales

An opportunity represents prospective, pending and closed "deals" or gifts.  This entity allows nonprofit organizations to track their efforts to build relationships with prospective donors.  
  
 Latest version of the JSON entity definition is available on <a href="https://github.com/Microsoft/CDM/tree/master/schemaDocuments/core/applicationCommon/foundationCommon/crmCommon/accelerators/nonProfit/nonProfitForSales/Opportunity.cdm.json" target="_blank">GitHub</a>.

This value is copied from associated Campaign at gift creation, and can be manually changed if necessary.|<a href="Opportunity.md" target="_blank">nonProfitForSales/Opportunity</a>|
|[solicitationType_display](#solicitationType_display)||<a href="Opportunity.md" target="_blank">nonProfitForSales/Opportunity</a>|
|[sourceCode](#sourceCode)|Organization defined unique code for associated Campaign. This value is copied from associated Campaign at gift creation.|<a href="Opportunity.md" target="_blank">nonProfitForSales/Opportunity</a>|

### <a href=#closeProbability name="closeProbability">closeProbability</a>

Type a number from 0 to 100 that represents the likelihood of closing the opportunity. This can aid the sales team in their efforts to convert the opportunity in a sale.  
First included in: nonProfitForSales/Opportunity (this entity)

### <a href=#sourceCode name="sourceCode">sourceCode</a>

Organization defined unique code for associated Campaign. This value is copied from associated Campaign at gift creation.  
First included in: nonProfitForSales/Opportunity (this entity)
